  <a id="3311" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="3313" href="foundation.type-arithmetic-empty-type.html#7685" class="Function">map-right-unit-law-coprod-is-empty</a><a id="3347" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="3477" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="3482" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="3489" href="foundation.universe-levels.html" class="Module">foundation.universe-levels</a> <a id="3516" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="3522" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3523" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="3528" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="3530" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a><a id="3532" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="3534" href="Agda.Primitive.html#764" class="Primitive">lzero</a><a id="3539" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="3541" href="Agda.Primitive.html#780" class="Primitive">lsuc</a><a id="3545" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="3547" href="Agda.Primitive.html#810" class="Primitive Operator">_⊔_</a><a id="3550" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="4109" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#4549" class="Function">is-not-contractible-Fin</a><a id="4132" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="4134" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7668" class="Function">succ-Fin</a><a id="4142" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="4144" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#4439" class="Function">is-contr-Fin-one-ℕ</a><a id="4162" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
## Idea

2-element types are types that are merely equivalent to the standard 2-element type `Fin 2`.

## Definition

### The condition that a type has two elements

<pre class="Agda"><a id="has-two-elements-Prop"></a><a id="4343" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4343" class="Function">has-two-elements-Prop</a> <a id="4365" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4367" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4368" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4368" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4370" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4372" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4377" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4379" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4381" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4384" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4368" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4386" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4388" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#1380" class="Function">UU-Prop</a> <a id="4396" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4368" class="Bound">l</a>
<a id="4398" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4343" class="Function">has-two-elements-Prop</a> <a id="4420" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4420" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="4422" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4424" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4862" class="Function">has-cardinality-Prop</a> <a id="4445" class="Number">2</a> <a id="4447" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4420" class="Bound">X</a>

<a id="has-two-elements"></a><a id="4450" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4450" class="Function">has-two-elements</a> <a id="4467" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4469" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4470" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4470" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4472" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4474" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4479" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4481" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4483" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4486" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4470" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4488" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4490" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4493" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4470" class="Bound">l</a>
<a id="4495" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4450" class="Function">has-two-elements</a> <a id="4512" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4512" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="4514" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4516" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#1482" class="Function">type-Prop</a> <a id="4526" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4527" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4343" class="Function">has-two-elements-Prop</a> <a id="4549" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4512" class="Bound">X</a><a id="4550" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="is-prop-has-two-elements"></a><a id="4553" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4553" class="Function">is-prop-has-two-elements</a> <a id="4578" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4580" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4581" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4581" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4583" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4585" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4590" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4592" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4593" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4593" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="4595" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4597" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4600" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4581" class="Bound">l</a><a id="4601" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4603" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4605" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#1295" class="Function">is-prop</a> <a id="4613" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4614" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4450" class="Function">has-two-elements</a> <a id="4631" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4593" class="Bound">X</a><a id="4632" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="4634" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4553" class="Function">is-prop-has-two-elements</a> <a id="4659" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4660" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4660" class="Bound">l</a><a id="4661" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4663" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4664" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4664" class="Bound">X</a><a id="4665" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4667" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4669" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#1549" class="Function">is-prop-type-Prop</a> <a id="4687" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4688" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4343" class="Function">has-two-elements-Prop</a> <a id="4710" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4664" class="Bound">X</a><a id="4711" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### The type of all 2-element types of universe level `l`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="2-Element-Type"></a><a id="4785" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4785" class="Function">2-Element-Type</a> <a id="4800" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4802" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4803" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4803" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4805" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4807" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4812" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4814" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4816" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4819" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4820" href="Agda.Primitive.html#780" class="Primitive">lsuc</a> <a id="4825" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4803" class="Bound">l</a><a id="4826" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="4828" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4785" class="Function">2-Element-Type</a> <a id="4843" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4843" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4845" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4847" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5153" class="Function">UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="4860" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4843" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4862" class="Number">2</a>

<a id="type-2-Element-Type"></a><a id="4865" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4865" class="Function">type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="4885" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4887" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4888" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4888" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4890" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4892" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4897" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4899" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4901" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4785" class="Function">2-Element-Type</a> <a id="4916" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4888" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4918" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4920" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4923" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4888" class="Bound">l</a>
<a id="4925" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4865" class="Function">type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="4945" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4947" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a>

<a id="has-two-elements-type-2-Element-Type"></a><a id="4952" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4952" class="Function">has-two-elements-type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="4989" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="4993" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4994" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4994" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4996" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4998" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="5003" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5005" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5006" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5006" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="5008" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5010" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4785" class="Function">2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5025" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4994" class="Bound">l</a><a id="5026" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5028" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5030" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4450" class="Function">has-two-elements</a> <a id="5047" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5048" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4865" class="Function">type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5068" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5006" class="Bound">X</a><a id="5069" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="5071" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4952" class="Function">has-two-elements-type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5108" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5110" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a>
</pre>
## Properties

### The condition of having two elements is closed under equivalences

<pre class="Agda"><a id="5213" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="5220" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5220" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="5224" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5225" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5225" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="5228" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5228" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="5231" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5233" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="5238" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5240" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5241" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5241" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="5243" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5245" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="5248" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5225" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="5250" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5252" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5253" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5253" class="Bound">Y</a> <a id="5255" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5257" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="5260" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5228" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="5262" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="5266" class="Keyword">where</a>
  
  <a id="5277" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5277" class="Function">has-two-elements-equiv</a> <a id="5300" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5302" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5241" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="5304" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1607" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="5306" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5253" class="Bound">Y</a> <a id="5308" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5310" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4450" class="Function">has-two-elements</a> <a id="5327" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5241" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="5329" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5331" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4450" class="Function">has-two-elements</a> <a id="5348" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5253" class="Bound">Y</a>
  <a id="5352" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5277" class="Function">has-two-elements-equiv</a> <a id="5375" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5375" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="5377" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5377" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="5379" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5381" href="foundation.mere-equivalences.html#2248" class="Function">transitive-mere-equiv</a> <a id="5403" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5377" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="5405" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5406" href="foundation.propositional-truncations.html#2096" class="Function">unit-trunc-Prop</a> <a id="5422" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5375" class="Bound">e</a><a id="5423" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="5428" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5428" class="Function">has-two-elements-equiv&#39;</a> <a id="5452" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5454" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5241" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="5456" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1607" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="5458" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5253" class="Bound">Y</a> <a id="5460" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5462" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4450" class="Function">has-two-elements</a> <a id="5479" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5253" class="Bound">Y</a> <a id="5481" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5483" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4450" class="Function">has-two-elements</a> <a id="5500" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5241" class="Bound">X</a>
  <a id="5504" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5428" class="Function">has-two-elements-equiv&#39;</a> <a id="5528" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5528" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="5530" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5530" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="5532" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="5538" href="foundation.mere-equivalences.html#2248" class="Function">transitive-mere-equiv</a> <a id="5560" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5530" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="5562" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5563" href="foundation.propositional-truncations.html#2096" class="Function">unit-trunc-Prop</a> <a id="5579" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5580" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#5707" class="Function">inv-equiv</a> <a id="5590" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5528" class="Bound">e</a><a id="5591" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
### Any 2-element type is inhabited

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-inhabited-2-Element-Type"></a><a id="5644" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5644" class="Function">is-inhabited-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5672" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="5676" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5677" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5677" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="5679" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5681" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="5686" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5688" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5689" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5689" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="5691" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5693" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4785" class="Function">2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5708" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5677" class="Bound">l</a><a id="5709" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5711" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5713" href="foundation.propositional-truncations.html#2012" class="Function">type-trunc-Prop</a> <a id="5729" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5730" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4865" class="Function">type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5750" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5689" class="Bound">X</a><a id="5751" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="5753" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5644" class="Function">is-inhabited-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5781" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5781" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="5783" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="5787" href="foundation.propositional-truncations.html#5581" class="Function">apply-universal-property-trunc-Prop</a>

    <a id="5915" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5917" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="5919" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5919" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="5921" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5923" href="foundation.propositional-truncations.html#2096" class="Function">unit-trunc-Prop</a> <a id="5939" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5940" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1807" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="5950" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5919" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="5952" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7083" class="Function">zero-Fin</a><a id="5960" class="Symbol">))</a>

#### Completing the characterization of the identity type of the type of 2-element types of arbitrary universe level

### For any 2-element type `X`, the type of automorphisms on `X` is a 2-element type.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="16301" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="16308" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#16308" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="16312" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16313" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#16313" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="16315" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16317" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="16322" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16324" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16325" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#16325" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="16327" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16329" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4785" class="Function">2-Element-Type</a> <a id="16344" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#16313" class="Bound">l</a><a id="16345" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="16349" class="Keyword">where</a>
  
  <a id="16360" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#16360" class="Function">has-two-elements-Aut-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="16396" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="16402" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4450" class="Function">has-two-elements</a> <a id="16419" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16420" href="foundation.automorphisms.html#1210" class="Function">Aut</a> <a id="16424" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16425" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4865" class="Function">type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="16445" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#16325" class="Bound">X</a><a id="16446" class="Symbol">))</a>
  <a id="16451" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#16360" class="Function">has-two-elements-Aut-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="16487" class="Symbol">=</a>

### The canonical type family on the type of 2-element types has no section

### Any automorphism on `Fin 2` is an involution

### The swapping equivalence on arbitrary 2-element types

<pre class="Agda"><a id="22132" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="22139" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#22139" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="22143" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22144" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#22144" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="22146" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22148" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="22153" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22155" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22156" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#22156" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="22158" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22160" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4785" class="Function">2-Element-Type</a> <a id="22175" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#22144" class="Bound">l</a><a id="22176" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="22180" class="Keyword">where</a>

### The swapping equivalence is not the identity equivalence

<pre class="Agda"><a id="24045" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="24052" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#24052" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="24056" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24057" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#24057" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="24059" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24061" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="24066" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24068" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24069" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#24069" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="24071" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24073" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4785" class="Function">2-Element-Type</a> <a id="24088" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#24057" class="Bound">l</a><a id="24089" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="24093" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="24102" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#24102" class="Function">is-not-identity-equiv-precomp-equiv-equiv-succ-Fin</a> <a id="24153" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="24159" href="foundation-core.negation.html#452" class="Function">¬</a> <a id="24161" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24163" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#641" class="Datatype">Id</a> <a id="24166" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24168" href="foundation.equivalences.html#17649" class="Function">equiv-precomp-equiv</a> <a id="24188" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24189" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#11858" class="Function">equiv-succ-Fin</a> <a id="24204" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24205" class="Number">2</a><a id="24206" class="Symbol">})</a> <a id="24209" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24210" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4865" class="Function">type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="24230" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#24069" class="Bound">X</a><a id="24231" class="Symbol">))</a>
           <a id="24245" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24247" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#2480" class="Function">id-equiv</a><a id="24255" class="Symbol">))</a>

### Any Σ-type over `Fin 2` is a coproduct

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-coprod-Σ-Fin-two-ℕ"></a><a id="28956" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#28956" class="Function">is-coprod-Σ-Fin-two-ℕ</a> <a id="28978" class="Symbol">:</a>

### For any equivalence `e : Fin 2 ≃ X`, any element of `X` is either `e 0` or it is `e 1`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="29355" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="29362" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#29362" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="29366" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="29367" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#29367" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="29369" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29371" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="29376" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="29378" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29379" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#29379" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="29381" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29383" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4785" class="Function">2-Element-Type</a> <a id="29398" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#29367" class="Bound">l</a><a id="29399" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="29403" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="29412" class="Keyword">abstract</a>
    <a id="29425" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#29425" class="Function">is-contr-decide-value-equiv-Fin-two-ℕ</a> <a id="29463" class="Symbol">:</a>
      <a id="29471" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29472" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#29472" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="29474" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29476" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="29480" class="Number">2</a> <a id="29482" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1607" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="29484" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4865" class="Function">type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="29504" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#29379" class="Bound">X</a><a id="29505" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29507" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29508" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#29508" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="29510" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29512" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4865" class="Function">type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="29532" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#29379" class="Bound">X</a><a id="29533" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29535" class="Symbol">→</a>
